ZXVRAM:4000             ; Memory Map:
ZXVRAM:4000             ;
ZXVRAM:4000             ; $4000-$57FF - spectrum video memory
ZXVRAM:4000             ; $5800-$5AFF - spectrum attribute memory
ZXVRAM:4000             ; $5B00-$6287 - variables
ZXVRAM:4000             ; $6288-$D1EA - code and data
ZXVRAM:4000             ; $D200-$D9FF - video buffer
ZXVRAM:4000             ;       $F0FF - stack
ZXVRAM:4000             ; $F100-$FFFF - bit-shift & bit-reverse lookup tables
ZXVRAM:4000             ;             - (built at run-time)
ZXVRAM:4000
ZXVRAM:4000

ZXVRAM:4000             ; Target assembler: ASxxxx by Alan R. Baldwin v1.5
